				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Pièces de clavecin avec une méthode (Rameau, Jean-Philippe)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>

<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1724 (revised 1731)
</td></tr>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP339473" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_18">

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Pièces de clavecin avec une méthode
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Pièces de Clavessin avec une Méthode pour la Méchanique des Doigts.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Rameau,_Jean-Philippe" title="Category:Rameau, Jean-Philippe">Rameau, Jean-Philippe</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>RCT 2-4
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>None <small>[<span class="icatassign">force assignment</span>]</small>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>20 pieces (2 suites); the divisions of "suite" and the numbering are not original.
<ul><li>Menuet en Rondeau, RCT 4 (exemple de doigtés en ut; ne fait pas partie de la suite en Mi)
</li></ul>
<dl><dt><ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Suite_in_E_minor,_RCT_2_(Rameau,_Jean-Philippe)" title="Suite in E minor, RCT 2 (Rameau, Jean-Philippe)">Suite in E minor, RCT 2</a></i>
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Allemande
</dd><dd>2. Courante
</dd><dd>3. Gigue en Rondeau
</dd><dd>4. Le rappel des Oiseaux
</dd><dd>5. 1er &amp; 2me Rigaudon
</dd><dd>6. Double du 2me Rigaudon
</dd><dd>7. Musette en Rondeau
</dd><dd>8. Tambourin
</dd><dd>9. La villageoise (Rondeau)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li><i>Suite in D major, RCT 3</i>
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>10. Les tendres plaintes (Rondeau)
</dd><dd>11. Les niais de Sologne
<dl><dd>a. 1er double des Niais
</dd><dd>b. 2me double des Niais
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>12. Les soupirs
</dd><dd>13. La joyeuse (Rondeau)
</dd><dd>14. La follette (Rondeau)
</dd><dd>15. L'Entretien des Muses
</dd><dd>16. Les tourbillons (Rondeau)
</dd><dd>17. Les cyclopes (Rondeau)
</dd><dd>18. Le lardon (Menuet)
</dd><dd>19. La boiteuse
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1724 (revised 1731)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>harpsichord
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Related Works
</th>
<td>Tambourin (No.8) was orchestrated for Act III, Scene 7 of <i><a href="/wiki/Les_f%C3%AAtes_d%27H%C3%A9b%C3%A9_(Rameau,_Jean-Philippe)" title="Les fêtes d'Hébé (Rameau, Jean-Philippe)" class="mw-redirect">Les fêtes d'Hébé</a></i>.<br />Le lardon (No.18) serves as the theme for<br /><i><a href="/wiki/Variations,_interlude_et_final_sur_un_th%C3%A8me_de_Rameau_(Dukas,_Paul)" title="Variations, interlude et final sur un thème de Rameau (Dukas, Paul)">Variations, interlude et final sur un thème de Rameau</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Category:Dukas,_Paul" title="Category:Dukas, Paul">Paul Dukas</a>.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pi%C3%A8ces_de_Clavecin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pièces de Clavecin">Wikipedia article</a>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
